[02-Mar-23 10:10 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Kovus**:	All data for FIO (including chat) is captured by a browser extension running on a lot of different people's computers.  At some point, due to Chrome getting pickier about MV2 & MV3 extensions, some functionality in the published extension was disabled, and thus chat for this particular channel was no longer being sent to FIO.


[02-Mar-23 10:12 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Kovus**:	I have an experimental (unpublished) extension that is MV3 compatible, which does send this channel's chat.  Because it's not yet complete, it's not published.  Therefore, it's only running on a couple systems, so it requires at least one of them to be online in order to send this channel's chat.  (Which is then used by the UFO Bot to verify users in discord against their PrUn id).


[02-Mar-23 10:12 AM] ApexChat#8127
**Kovus**:	Hence, the purpose of this channel is to provide a way for people to verify their discord account to their in game user. It is currently only used for the UFO Discord: https://discord.gg/vwcUJx8HHP
